# Text Elements
It is both complete and a binary tree. Each child has two nodes except the leaf nodes,
and all layers are completely full except the bottom layer ^aZ4MQzok

(See problem 1) ^P5zAit5x

Heaps may be effeciently stored in arrays, since they have no empty nodes, or un-even branches,
allowing us to operate quickly on them ^JnCapMA2

Priority queues are queues that have priority assosiated with their members.
Only the member with the "highest" priority is returned when requested ^JBTR9pXs

On heaps, we can insert, and remove items from the user's side as basic operations,
but on our backend we use reheapUp and reheapDown, to perform those operations, in order
to maintain our heap requirements ^Uwq6hn8j
